console:
========
{
  let json, data

  json = document.querySelector('script#__NEXT_DATA__[type="application/json"]')
  json = json.innerText
  json = JSON.parse(json)

  try {
    if (json.props.pageProps.aboveTheFoldData.titleType.isEpisode) {
      data = {
        series_id: json.props.pageProps.aboveTheFoldData.series.series.id,
        season:    json.props.pageProps.aboveTheFoldData.series.episodeNumber.seasonNumber,
        episode:   json.props.pageProps.aboveTheFoldData.series.episodeNumber.episodeNumber
      }
    }
    else if (json.props.pageProps.aboveTheFoldData.titleType.isSeries) {
      data = {
        series_id: json.props.pageProps.tconst,
        season:    null,
        episode:   null
      }
    }
    else {
      data = {
        movie_id: json.props.pageProps.tconst
      }
    }

    console.log(
      JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)
    )
  }
  catch(e) {
    console.log(e.message)
  }
}

console:
========
{
  let json, data

  json = document.querySelector('script#__NEXT_DATA__[type="application/json"]')
  json = json.innerText
  json = JSON.parse(json)

  try {
    if (json.props.pageProps.aboveTheFoldData.titleType.isEpisode) {
      data = {
        series_id: json.props.pageProps.aboveTheFoldData.series.series.id,
        season:    json.props.pageProps.aboveTheFoldData.series.episodeNumber.seasonNumber,
        episode:   json.props.pageProps.aboveTheFoldData.series.episodeNumber.episodeNumber
      }
    }
    else if (json.props.pageProps.aboveTheFoldData.titleType.isSeries) {
      data = {
        series_id: json.props.pageProps.tconst,
        season:    null,
        episode:   null
      }
    }
    else {
      data = {
        movie_id: json.props.pageProps.tconst
      }
    }

    console.log(
      JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)
    )
  }
  catch(e) {
    console.log(e.message)
  }
}
